 Samajwadi Party founder Mulayam Singh Yadav is filing nomination from Uttar Pradesh's Mainpuri Lok Sabha seat today
 yani 2019 kii chunavi jang main mulaayam singh us loksabhaa kshetra se bhagya aajamaa rahe hai jahaan se vijay praapt karte hue unhone apni sansadeey raajnneeti kaa aagaaj kiya tha
 23 years ago in 1996, Mulayam Singh Yadav reached Lok Sabha only after winning the first Lok Sabha election of his life from Mainpuri seat
 itnaa hi nahin, is chunaav main vijay pataakaa lahraane vaale mulaayam singh yadav ko centre main bani sanyukt morche kii sarkaar main raksha mantralay sanbhaalane kii ahm jimmedaari bhi mili thi

 umr ke aath dashak puure kar rahe mulaayam singh yadav ko siyaasi akhaade kaa bada pahalwaan mana jaataa he or unke bete akhilesh yadav ne samaajawaadee party kii siyasat ko usee raah par laa diya he, jis par kabhi mulaayam singh yadav ne apni manzil pai thi
 After the collapse of the Babri Masjid structure across the country, the politics of mandal-kamandal started, in which Mulayam Singh Yadav tied up his newly formed party with Bahujan Samaj Party and the 1993 UP Assembly elections were fought by both parties together
 mulaayam singh kii yah tarkeeb kaam kar gai or vah upi ke mukhyamantri bane

 When Mulayam Singh became the defense minister, a United Front government was formed in the center and Mulayam Singh Yadav was the defense minister between 1996-1998
 haalanki, yah sarkaar zyada din nahin chali or ek baar halaat ye paidaa ho gaye ki mulaayam singh yadav kaa naam pradhanmantri kii res main bhi aane laga

 iske baad 1998 main chunaav hue to mulaayam singh ne sanbhal seat se baaji ladi or jeet hasil kii

 baad main unhone kannauj seat apane bete akhilesh yadav ke liye chhod di, jahaan hue upachunaav main wo pehali baar saansad bane

 jiske baad 2004 main hue upachunaav main mulaayam ke bhattije dharmendra yadav yahaan se jite or 2014 main mulaayam singh ke pote tej pratap singh yadav ne upachunaav main yahaan se jeet darj kii
 Mulayam Singh kept the Azamgarh seat with him
